name:Yâ€oâ€uâ€xâ€iâ€aâ€oâ€gâ€uâ€aâ€i
info:Garden-view Twin Room
info:Stayed in February 2024
info:Family
info:8 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted February 20, 2024
msg:A very satisfying experience. A family of three traveled. The child was in junior high school. We bought a three-person package for 2,000 yuan, which included three Yunhai Hot Spring tickets (unlimited entry), three Fantasy Valley tickets (unlimited entry), three buffet breakfasts, and three interstellar tickets (there seemed to be a children's buffet dinner, which was wasted). I arrived at the hotel at noon on the first day. After swiping my ID card at the front desk, I could go directly to Fantasy Valley to play. After recording my face, I could enter Fantasy Valley and Hot Springs unlimited times for two days. It was very convenient to scan my face. The quick pass of Fantasy Valley is 180 per person, including 8 projects. We didn't buy it. The difficult projects can basically be swiped into the park half an hour in advance the next morning through the fast entry channel. There are self-service drinks and ice cream in the hot spring. You can go in and drink them if you are thirsty. You have to pay for food (the sign is not obvious, and we didn't find it until the next day). The hotel is very new, the rooms and facilities are good, and the breakfast is average. Overall, it is a very low-cost happiness during the Chinese New Year.

posted:Posted February 13, 2024
msg:It takes about 4 hours to drive from Wuhan to Xiangyang OCT. Ctrip booked a garden view room at OCT Yunhai Hotel (including Yunhai Hot Spring tickets for 3 people + 2-day unlimited admission tickets for 3 people in Fantasy Valley + 3-day breakfast for Star Adventure) ğŸ’°2017 yuan. The price is more expensive during the Chinese New Year than usual. The above room + ticket is only about ğŸ’°1480 for off-season travel. Tourists staying in the hotel can enter Fantasy Valley half an hour in advance. Fantasy Valley is a 5-minute walk to the right of the hotel. The hotel also has a free shuttle bus. The first floor of the hotel can directly enter the hot spring, which is very convenient. There is a super large fish tank in the hotel lobby. You can sit in the restaurant and watch various fish and turtles in the underwater world, which is very suitable for children. However, the breakfast of the hotel in the peak season is simply hard to describe. There is no seat, no food, and no tableware. In fact, this breakfast can solve the problem by eating in different time periods. They are all concentrated in the 9-9:30 time period. It is overcrowded and there is no flow limit. There is no experience, which wears out the good impression of the first day.
